      ,TransFlag   = '1'                   
      ,ResultID    = '501'
      ,ResultDate  = '2021-05-22'
      ,ResultTime  = '13:26:40'
 Where SPECIMENNUM = '2105220011'  
   AND OrderCode   = '2015'    
   And LabCode     = '2015'   
   And TRANSFLAG   < '2'

   Set JStatus = '2'                       
 Where SPECIMENNUM  = '2105220011'

   AND Receiptdate = '2021-05-22'
